The first player to do so wins. To enter a piece into play from its yard to its starting square, a player must roll a 6. If a player has no pieces in play they get 3 tries to get a 6. Once a player has one or more pieces in play, he selects a piece and moves it forward along the track the number of squares indicated by the die roll.
